A grand castle-like building with these key features:

Main structure approximately 50 blocks wide, 30 blocks deep, and 40 blocks tall
Walls made of gray stone bricks
Steep triangular roof made of dark oak planks, with three distinct peaks
Central peak slightly taller and wider than the two flanking peaks
Large arched entrance at the center of the ground floor
Multiple floors with symmetrically placed windows (3x2 blocks each)
Circular stained glass window in the central roof peak
Surrounding stone brick wall enclosure, approximately 5 blocks tall
Patterned pathway leading to the main entrance, made of stone, andesite, and other light-colored blocks
Landscaped courtyard inside the wall enclosure with trees and custom vegetation

Interior features:

Grand entrance hall with vaulted ceiling
Colorful carpet runners in blue, green, red, and white
Stone brick walls with leaf block and vine decorations
Glowstone chandeliers hanging from the ceiling
Multiple rooms branching off from the main hall, including a library with bookshelves
Wooden flooring in some areas, stone brick in others
Large windows allowing natural light

Provide step-by-step instructions on how to construct this elaborate castle, including exact dimensions, block types, and placement of windows, doors, and decorative elements. Describe the roof construction, interior layout, and how to create the surrounding wall and landscape. Include details on interior decoration, such as the colorful carpet design, chandelier placement, and how to integrate nature elements inside the structure. Ensure the description captures both the imposing exterior and the intricate, welcoming interior of the building.
